[广东顺德人权捍卫者李碧云自述所遭遇的人权侵害](https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/06/blog-post_91.html)
------

<div>
<span></span><span><a name='more'></a></span><div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"><a href="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhjMT3nh8Db7o_RUxpSwmEDYsqnSm0xCnfbvTUVK8gFhgmvOCKw2x39XWRQTLpnqbTNif9HtGeSKs5ntnpxRwG9igvnCrm0uPrbKLDZIMZJ51s3Xnp2-NSzBLszgMlDmZIW7mLhE43L7WTS71ORHS8Pgrz5SHYjUc_S-Pp6ViYUqd_SPCyIrMzPlnLmLIn6/s1280/LiBiyun.jpeg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" data-original-height="1280" data-original-width="720" height="640" src="https://blogger.googleusercontent.com/img/b/R29vZ2xl/AVvXsEhjMT3nh8Db7o_RUxpSwmEDYsqnSm0xCnfbvTUVK8gFhgmvOCKw2x39XWRQTLpnqbTNif9HtGeSKs5ntnpxRwG9igvnCrm0uPrbKLDZIMZJ51s3Xnp2-NSzBLszgMlDmZIW7mLhE43L7WTS71ORHS8Pgrz5SHYjUc_S-Pp6ViYUqd_SPCyIrMzPlnLmLIn6/w360-h640/LiBiyun.jpeg" width="360" /></a></div><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">【李碧云：敬请省委省政府下令顺德区委区政府领导，容桂街办领导吴磊，原容桂街办书记刘国兴（现顺德区政府副主席）容里居委会村官梁敏英，蔡景薪容桂派出所等有关领导停止单一对残疾李碧云和亲人一切刁难侵害，还我人身自由权和医疗权，让我能享有坐地铁、的的汽车、高铁等交通工具的权利，让社会文明家国和谐</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 楷体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">特向各机关部门公布！也向各界媒体，律师界、国际人权组织、女权机构、社会大众公布！请帮助李碧云！】<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">特别声明：已</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年了，中国这人权比美国人权好五倍的大国。一个普通的弱女子李碧云遭广东顺德政府公检法权势侵犯人权，被多宗多宗枉法构罪判刑，十年之久的住房和店铺被强拆失去经济收入与栖身之处，官司胜诉了失去自由，亲姐被害死了等株连迫害、多次被绑架歹毒酷刑凌辱迫供暴殴身体成半残生活不能自理还不罢休，还被顺德政府滥用职权</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">权大于法</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">继续仗势欺压用卑劣、阴险、暴殴、威胁、拦截、绑架、抢劫、关押、虐待等咬住不放，还派数十人每日</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">小时看守监视限制人身自由和剥夺医疗权。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2024</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年元旦日，半残李碧云在顺德大良街道钟楼公园想乘坐</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号地铁，而看守人对接顺德政府容桂街道掌权人的发号令，而我落地铁扶手电梯时就被这帮人实施撞、拉，围堵，用屁股顶撞等凌辱卑劣行为撞我半残身体而昏，这是中国政府的耻辱；（若肢体活动受阻李碧云人身再受任何伤害或其他生命伤害等任何伤人事故、与李碧云亲人的人身受到任何交通事故或其他伤害都是有关顺德区委区政府领导，容桂街办领导吴磊，江定东、蔡景新、原容桂街办书记刘国兴（现顺德区政府副主席）容里居委会村官梁敏英，胡祺昌、容桂派出所所长等公权部门领导对我而言滥权所作所为到极致，无法用文字来形容。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">国家发展为富裕民生生活是好的。源于顺德区委区政府借《广东省委、省政府在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1999</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月广东省委、省政府确定为<u>率先基本实现现代化试点之后（简称</u>试点方案）<u>》</u>，但顺德政府容桂街道办等政府参与组织官员起了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">邪念的欲望</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">将容里村民辛苦积累的庞大物业资金土地资源成了腐官员的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">狼中物</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，将容里村本是一个已经<u>率先</u>富裕村试成返贫村。农民挣的血汉钱确实不容易！村民怨声载道，多次站出来依法维护宪法法律就是维护自已合法权益也被镇压被打被行拘。于在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2008</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年村民发现建设</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容桂站</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的工程</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">太澳高筑公路</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">广珠轻轨</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">佛山至顺德的快速干线的施工路段占用容里村民农田</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">被地方政府官以权侵吞征地款，集体村民维权行动再次兴起。在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年期间我无意拍到维权村民被暴打的视频交给受伤村民了，后参与容里村集体土地维权，提了一条合理化建议并说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">希望容里村民皆大欢喜</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">惹得个别领导不悦；与此，也被村委与容桂街办等组织带军人穿制服入村迫村民签名，甚至出动几千警力镇压村民与抓捕维权村民，而我李碧云成了容里居委会村官梁敏英等组织为卖容里村土地谋私利串谋顺德政府公检法齐上实施打击迫害</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">杀鸡儆猴</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">来镇压维权村民为达目的（三番五次重复性嫁祸罪名妨碍公务罪，破坏选举罪，盗窃罪等判罪，将我十年之久的栖身住房和经济收入被违法强拆，造成我居无定所），官司胜诉了未得到赔偿，如同一张白纸</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">权大于法，还被容桂街道书记刘国兴，村官梁敏英，蔡景薪等腐败官滥用职权徇私枉法派出雇佣兵每日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">小时看守、监视，寄姐妹家跟到哪，汇报行踪，拦截绑架限制李碧云人身自由和剥夺医疗权等有持无恐，迫害株连家人亲姐而死等迫害为目的来镇压容里村民出来维权</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">追溯到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日，容里村民委托我和几个村民到广东省公安厅反映诉求问题，不料，我们出省厅门口被跨市容桂民警李志堃带</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7-8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">拦截，选择性将我手无缚鸡之力民女李碧云绑架暴打刑逼供，一个普通普通的村弱女李碧云说真话被地方政府官为侵吞容里村民征地补偿和圈占土地，就被视</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">眼中盯</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">连锁暴殴报复致残构罪妨碍公务罪判</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个月；因</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2011</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多村民投票选容里村委主任而被当局排除了，在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2011</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">626</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个容里村民推存我参选人大选举，当局被迫将我列入侯选人之一，而我</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2011</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">20</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被当局就要冤枉我构</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">破坏选举罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">等一直针对咬住挡</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">箭巴</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">来镇压维权村民。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2013</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年期间村民表决诉求分宅基地自建房，我在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2013</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被绑架刑拘</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">14</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">天妨碍公务罪。梁敏英卖容里村民土地款不给村民，我在家睡觉被构罪妨碍公务罪等。将我十年之久栖身之所的住房和经济收入的店铺在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">28</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被违法强拆了。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日李碧云出狱后进行行复议，贏了官司失去自由，反被容桂街办书记刘国兴、容桂公安、容里村官梁敏英等组织滥权灭人性搞政绩维稳的旗号持久年剥夺李碧云人身自由权和医疗权，亲姐被害死还不罢休等，正因侵吞卖容里村几百亩土地款与高额</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">维稳费</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的驱动下有持无恐一一就在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被顺德政府、容桂街办掌权人刘国兴和容里村官梁敏委派容桂公安蔡景薪等半百穿制服跨大良街道借传呼到妹民宅破门抢劫民财，毁证据绑架伤人，刘国兴还不消气于</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日下令数百人恃武器惨剧伤人抢劫绑架等强拆妹民宅，同年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">25</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">将李碧云家人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">人行政拘留。就</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">25</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日按法院通知到广州铁路法院途中将李碧云妹李彩云弟李添强被绑架连锁构罪盗窃罪与李碧云再构妨碍公务罪，被强行稳人架起我身体前顶住、后用拳头拳拳暴打身体的脊椎脊拆而昏等，关押期间派人单一针对对我一个残废人撞踢落地而昏，撞落梯级而昏，推落厕所马桶、拖落数层楼梯级，踢拆腰椎，天寒地冻不被棉衣，被子抽落冷硬硬的地砖上而中风，等等歹毒行为，将李碧云身体刑暴残酷虐待刑废到生活不能自理</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2022</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日伤瘫李碧云穿着</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">纸尿裤</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">刑满释放了，新官的容桂街办掌权人党委书记兼区副书记吴磊，江定东、欧胜军与科长吴湛华、原维稳主任何文洪等领导承诺依法合理赔偿而出尔反尔未采取实施行动<span lang="EN-GB">,</span>反而滥权欺压非法指使数拾所谓工作员以监控、围堵、殴打、拦截、绑架、抢劫、盗窃、恐吓，残害限制李碧云人身自由权和剥夺医疗权等方式实施身体、精神等侵害行为。无道德的底线迫害，践踏宪法、耻辱了中国政府，这样对待一老残弱女是法治政府吗？<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">14</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年多了李碧云遭受顺德区政府、公、检、法的多宗枉判，多次酷刑残暴刑废我李碧云，确得不到公道，还被削夺医治；官司胜诉了，住房和店铺被强拆</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年多了未依法赔偿。如今</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2024</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年了，在迈向法治文明的中国，敬请中国政府国务院，中纪委，最高法院，最高检查院、公安部真正倾听基层老百姓的真实声音直接暗访直接现场督查调查，为李碧云和家人送来</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">人间温暖、点亮曙光</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">严惩地方政府公检法涉嫌违法违纪的公职人员，刹住</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">损民歪风</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">树立党的威信，确保政令畅通！<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">一，容里村八十年代末已实现了工业发展和城乡建设<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我是李碧云，出生是广东省佛山市顺德区容桂街道容里村村人（也是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4911</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">股权人之一），顺德一直是鱼米之乡，开放后工业更让迅速发展富裕起来，我高中毕业后一直在家乡工作，主要是从事财务工作，一直有优越稳定工作和生活。容里村是原容桂镇的一个行政大村，面积</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5.3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方公里（是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7950</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">亩），八十年代已兴建起</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里工业城</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">等（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">90</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年代已租金收入近一亿，已有股份分红了），历年来，建设发展建设了道路</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">40</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公里，路宽</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">30-40</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">米，建设了开关站，水厂，小学，中心公园等。实现了工业发展和城乡建设。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> 2000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年末容里村集体积累储蓄资金</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">亿元了（附图</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）等，当年容里村已进入小康生活了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">; </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">也是一个</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">肥肉</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">之容里村。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（一），基本农田不是谁都能征收的，没有国务院审批就是违法。土地是农民的生存之本。据《基本农田保护条例》第五条规定：任何单位和个人不得改变或占用基本农田，确实需要要占用基本农田，涉及农田地转用或是征收土地的必须经国务院的批准。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">本来我有一个好端端的身体与小康生活。李碧云在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年期间到容桂街道容里居委会纠正父母</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">80</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年代建的民宅（房产证）被有关部门工作员失误将姓</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">写错姓</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">梁</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（意欲何为至今</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2024</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年了有关部门也不更正？）。目睹维权村民被身穿制服的施工方追打维权村民而报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，又被穿着迷理服百多人拿铁棒，铁铲，收缩棒暴打村民而拍到（视频给受伤二十村民有骨折）！而交给受伤村民，这是良心的仁德</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">与此之后，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">经许多村民的极力请求参与村民集体维权了，与此，我才知道</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4911</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个股权村民历年投资的容里村民辛苦积聚的物业资金土地资产被不知情下流失</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">给天富来</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的情况根源，从</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1999</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月被广东省委、省政府确定为率先基本实现现代代试点之后（简称</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">试点方案）；而（一个富裕的容里村被试成一个扶贫的容里返贫村）。。。。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">自改革开放以来，容里村八十年代末，确定</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">筑巢引凤，引凤筑巢</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的发展战略，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年，容里村民集体年末储蓄余额</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">亿元了，已是一个富裕行政村。而触动了顺德区容桂街办领导的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">邪恶心念</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，从</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2001</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年的顺德区容桂街道办党委书记邓伟根滥用职权和各届容里居委会村官村霸一把手赵元锐、关荣昌和任职</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">16</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年了如今梁敏英利用职务之便等各级官员侵吞</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里村集体</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的财政土地资金，真正谋取他们的个人的成团体的利益，实现了自已的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">首先富裕</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。这种恶劣的集体贪腐行为至今，没有被清算。各级官员参与推动</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">试点方案</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">对土地管理法律监管不到位、土地监管不严导致滋生腐败不择手段抢吞容里村民土地物业资产。从</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1999</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月被广东省委、省政府确定为率先基本实现现代代试点之后（简称</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">试点），然后，顺德区委，区政府抓住作为广东省率先基本实现现代代试点为总目标，率先在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2001</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">30</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日作出了《关于进一步深化农村集体改革的决定》【顺发（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2001</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">13</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号】和《关于调整农村集体土地管理制度的实施细则》【顺府办发</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(2001)85</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号文】落实股份社资产固化量化后的农村宅基地留用制表，给股民的宅基地指标</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">80</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方宅基地建房】，接着，顺德第一个村级工业区改造试点</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">——</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">就是【容里村】。上级放开了对于地方政府的严历限制，这就给了容桂街办以绝隹的借口，建立</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">土发公司</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">等各种小组，严重放任，纵容基层政府官与容里村级组织串通抢吞村民积累的物业资产土地资源，不遵守制定</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">试点方案</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的规则，使容里村民无论在经济上，还是民生上，没有解决容里村民的住房、医疗、养老，不能提高容里村民的生活水来，反而逐步一个行政富裕的容里村了（是小康村），却变成一个贫困村（返贫村）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">二，借</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">试点</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">用</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">注册资本</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">千万的公司</span></b><b><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span></b><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">有征收的主体吗？<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">毛泽东打天下分田分地给农民，农民的土地物业不能做主？按中华人民共和国《土地管理法》的法律法规规定，土地的流转，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">必须是村民自愿，不管任何人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">‘</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">任何单位都不能擅自做主，不光如此。如果咱们是在被迫，被威胁的情况签字是无效的，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">土地的流转不能超过规定的期限，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">只能限于农村的耕地，草地荒地这些领域，如改变土地用途的话，土地的流转所得的金钱归村民所有，村委会一毛钱也不能拿，那些敢私自截留吃拿卡要卡要的村委会等依法追究法律责任。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">从</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2001</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年由原容里村委书记关伟行被借故辞官后，在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2002</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月许，地方权力委派</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">土发中心</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的经理赵元锐到容里村当书记兼任村委主任；于是赵元锐到容里村把村的一切事务必须由他独签名才有效，称为一枝笔制度。以</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">村改居</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">广东省委，省政府确定现代化试点方案。未经容里村民</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4911</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个（投资的权权人）股东同意私盖公章用虚假手续骗取政府红头批文，将容里村土地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩和</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4911</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个村民（也是股权）集资建起的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">亩的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里工业城</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">被滥用职权变成</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容桂土地发展中心</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">偷天换日压榨成从天掉下来的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">天富来工业城</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（附件</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> &nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2003</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">31</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日编号容征（一）征收原容里村委集体土地合同，没有《土地管理法》的法律规定的征地批文就被</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">土发中心</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">以暗箱操作，无视法律之威严，秘密把容里村</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩（含</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">亩的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里工业城）农田土地和市值数百亿元的工业区商铺物业等所有资产一次性强抢，只注册资本</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">千万的公司</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">土发中心</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">来征收</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩土地，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩的工业区，村民年末储蓄余额</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">亿元等？不是强抢吗？地方权力、资本强势一方面給村民出示的地价是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">75</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">元</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">/</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方、绿化用地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">21</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">元</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">/</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方，同一天，又給天富来签订了《土地使用权转让协议》中的单价是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">210</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">元</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">/</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方，同时村民不知情秘密解散《容里村集体股份资产物业公司》和村属下五个农业股份合作社，赵元锐变成了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">‘</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">土霸王</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">’</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。而</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年容里村民集体年末储蓄余额</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">亿元的资金落入谁人的口袋里？</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4911</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个容里村民失地失业。物业资金被侵吞了，生活难以维持；破坏了村民正常的生活，制造了社会的不和谐。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（三）容里村民失地失业失财产讨公理<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">问题是冷峻的摆在哪里</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">村改居</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">）】</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">32</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">批复</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">批复就抢夺</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日从佛山市国土资源局发布</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">天上掉下</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">天富来</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">工业城敢叫日月换新天</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">——</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">佛山市顺德区天富来国际工业城。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个容里村民集体积累储蓄资金</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩就被私分了等？</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">真正谋取了他们的个人的成团体的利益，实现了自已的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">首先富裕</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">广东省的试点制定规则，顺德政府不履行依法执行，不作为。不实施《关于进一步深化农村集体改革的决定》【顺发（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2001</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">13</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号】和《关于调整农村集体土地管理制度的实施细则》连征收土地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15%</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的提留地都不留置村民使用，连</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">固化宅基地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">” [</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">顺府办</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222;
