mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号文</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">]</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的宅基地指标给村民</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">80</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方宅基地建房也没有实施分配！被征收的村民都是上有老下有小的。使容里村民怨声载道，激发几千村民出来依法维权</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">打倒贪官，还我土地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">浩浩荡荡</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2007</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日到顺德容桂街道办找领导说法，并分别上访县（区）、市、省人民政府，但三级政府对于解决问题，是一点诚意都没有的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">,</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">推三挡四</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">,</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">一直没有具体的答复</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">. </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">由于地方权力不闻不问，所以容里村民由</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">07</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月一直在康富来维权。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2008</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年期间，容里村居委会换届选举，村民投票选为村民办实事的村委领导的。但容桂街道办出动大量公安警力干涉村民现场选举并用录影机不停地录影村民，滥权公权力，采用强权无所不用其极！村民投票刚结束还未点票，被容桂公安抢走投票票箱过十日后。被容桂街办滥权滥警委任容里村民梁敏英上任容里居委会主任至如今</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">16</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年了。梁敏英上位利用职务之便配合每届容桂街办领导无法无天骗卖容里村集体土地资产了。梁敏英在非法权力加持力量成</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">一把手</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（也是黑村霸首长）说了算的<u>【村选举委员会长、治安办站长，综治办站长，容里村村支部书记，容里村社区服务主任、国土城建水利，扶贫褔利，曾是</u></span><u><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2011</span></u><u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年容里居委会人大代表】，从（</span></u><u><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2008</span></u><u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年至今</span></u><u><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2024</span></u><u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年了）十六年多了梁敏英任职</span></u><u><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span></u><u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">清如水</span></u><u><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span></u><u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">吗？</span></u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里村的雄厚资金物业收入土地资产去了哪？原容里村本是富裕村，却成了贫困村）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">失田地上年纪的村民捡垃圾来维持生计！希得到中央政府彻查还公道！<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><b><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">二，我遭迫害的源因：征地补偿款被侵吞、借征地圈地征地事实<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">农民是靠土地保障生活的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">,</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">地方政府以</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">村改居</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">没有出示《征用土地公告办法》《征地补偿安置公告》，没有制订保障农民的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">居有所住，老有所乐，老有所养</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">等社会保障养老的长期生活生存。只有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里居委会</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">与</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">土发中心</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">谈征用土地的事，一个</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里居委会</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">与一个地方权力委派的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">土发中心</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">有权强征土地的主体吗？村民没有享受应有的福利，希望中央相关部门督办查办还村民公道</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">！！！</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2008</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月经维权容里村民发现建设</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容桂站</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的工程</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">太澳高筑公路</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">广珠轻轨</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">佛山至顺德的快速干线的施工路段占用容里村民农田</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">村民没有得到任何补偿款等，百名村民到施工现场要求停止施工时，集体维权行动再次兴起。与此，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">16</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">27</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日维权村民举起</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公告</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">牌的内容是【此地块属容里未征地块，禁止施工</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">有权追究法律责任！（附图</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）】，要求施工单位出示（征地公告与征地被偿协议）。而几个村民被数拾拿长棒的施工方的人追打，我巧在场拍摄现场，被对方追打，我本人和几个村民报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">也一直无人处理和制止，村民问</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">你来做什么的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。穿着制服的卢能业所长（警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">192166</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）回答</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">你够他们打吗？我是来睇戏的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。警方也没有及时制止，更没有抓捕凶手</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。在这之后，我们向上级政府反映被征用却未经合法决策程序、无补偿的问题，一直没有得到任何的答复。村民们则从</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月份底开始在工地上搭棚守地。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">与此，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日太澳高筑</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">广珠轻轨</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">顺德的快速干线的施工路段再次强行施工，引发上千村民到场地，而村民近二十人被施工方和政府所雇用成的百多个穿着迷彩制服的青年拿住铁棒铁铲、电棒追打暴伤村民事件（附图</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">），而我拍摄留下证据，而被对方打，被村民挡住而轻伤，而将视频交给村民</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">警方一直没制止，也没有抓捕凶手，后经媒体等关注</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，当局迫于无奈，顺德区政府、容桂街办列书记，容里居委会领导等部门协商下，受伤村民名单【重伤有五个有骨碎，手腕骨列】等出证明，以容里居委会</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">名义</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">盖上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公章</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">受伤村民就可以到容桂街道任何一间公立医院就医（附件</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> &nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）！同时受伤村民的报销药费款由容桂街道容里民警中队填付（附件</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> &nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）。受伤村民要求顺德公安依法立案处理，但不立案处理</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">........<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">又</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">26</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日容里村民集体股份合作社的股东自集在村委大楼讨论征地补偿会议，突然闯进十多辆各式各样的车来，有警车、装甲车和民用载货便车，车牌用封口胶封着，从车跳出二三百身穿迷彩服，戴头盔，自称武警的人，容桂公安为居委会卖地清除障碍，派出公安身穿迷彩服跟随居委人员，容桂街办人员深入农民家家户户强迫村民签名卖地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">居委人员向村民介绍说：</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">穿迷彩服的是刑警，特警随时有权捉人（附下图）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">村民已经害怕被捉</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">又</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">16</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日，太澳高筑</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">广珠轻轨</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">----</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">顺德的快速干线的施工路段再次强行施工，引发上千村民到场制止，此后，中铁施工方竟然以阻止施工为由起诉了六名村民并民事赔偿，向他们提出数十万的赔偿（后</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2010</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年用权力迫六个村民撤诉私了）。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因此，容里村民依法上访，冲破了容里居委会主任梁敏英串通容桂街办的封锁障碍。一方得到省人民政府支持和协助，省政府责令顺德区政府派一个不低于局级的领导帮我容里村民解决问题，顺德区领导带领国土局的用地科，土地执法科官员与我村民协商了两次，问题解决有了进展，并约定第三次协商。为了知道村民民意诉求，其根据容里村民由</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4911</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">股权人积累的资产的与容里村民土地资源概况，连合法的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">固化宅地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">据</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&nbsp;[</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">顺府办</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(2001)85</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号文</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">]</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">区政府定下来的宅基地指标给村民</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">80</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方建房也没有分配！据</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1999</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月广东省委，省政府的试点，据《土地管理法》等法律法规总一方案诉求，得到村民民意有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3100</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多个村民签名诉求，下一次约谈时向政府提建议协调村民是这个村民诉求名单的</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里居委会要把村民集体经济组织的耕地物业资产非法转给土地发展商，村民表决不同意，因为这些土地留作集体发展，收益用于村民养老补贴、村民困难补贴和村民各种福利开支。村民站出来依法维权，从</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月开始起，当局被迫开始公告</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">白菜价</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">向维权村民支付补偿款，金额从每个股东</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">380</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">元，一路增长到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1250</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">元，再到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">万元，又到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">万元，最后提高到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">万，但是，当局始终回避土地征地的决策程序合法性问题。村民一方面受到黑社会殴打、袭击，即使捉了这些黑社会人员交给公安，不久就是公安便把人放走。另一方面公安又向村民发传票或拘捕村民，村民感觉到威胁，生命无保障，于是恐慌，不得已派代表向广东省公安厅投诉与举报反映问题。害人的人，那就更加深感惧怕一一广东省佛山市顺德区容桂街道容里居委会（原容里村民也是是股权之一）手无缚鸡之力的李碧云就是一个鲜活的例子，让人不寒而栗！</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">第一刑拘，仅仅因为集体维权，遭跨市绑架刑毁身体，被构陷</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">妨碍公务罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">判有期</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个月《（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2010</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）粤顺刑初字第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">00587</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号》来镇压维权容里村民（从此李碧云失去了健康的身体，又丢了财务工作了等）<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日经容里村民委托，我李碧云和几个村民到广东省公安厅依法实事</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">反映</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">问题（当日是领导接访日，约有二百多上访人）。于是向省厅领导反映并咨询几个问题</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">第一，什么情况下采用警界线？第二，什么情况下才能出动军队，入村镇压村民？同时把随身带的证据给领导睇：其一份</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公告</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">13</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日表决村民未通过，是侵占国家征地补偿款，又捆绑其它土地；其二</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公告</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">盖</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公章</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">证明是【此地块属容里未征地块，禁止施工</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">有权追究法律责任；其三，村民被暴伤近二十人图片与村民暴伤证据，暴伤二十个村民顺德公安不立案处理；非法强抢占容里村土地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩和</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">亩容里工业城，滥用职权肆意出动警力入村镇压。就省厅领导给回执号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">0003954</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号写</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">出警是否滥用？<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">当我李碧云和几个村民刚出广省省公安厅门口，就被跨市等候广东省公安厅门口的顺德区容桂公安李志堃霍炳潮，曾喜顺等</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7-8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">五大男粗的男人（当时穿便服，没出示工作证的）突把我们拦截两段，强制把我一人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">‘</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">针对</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">’</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">拖拽上便车，把我的长发往车里死拉，把我手反扣，有人按住我双肩，把我上半身胸部紧贴住一个肥大男人（就是李志堃）的大腿上，由人分别用膝盖，拳头狠毒地对着我脊椎骨，腰椎暴打（并说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">敬酒不喝，要喝罚酒</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">），每一拳打来的力都被脊椎、腰椎，肉体的五脏六腑尽受了，脊椎、腰椎骨被暴打折（出狱住院检查的诊断单）严重等，疼痛无法不能不喊叫救命，发出凄凉的哀求声请不要再打我</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">但是，一双手紧紧掐住我脖子的咽喉不能发出声音、造成声带严重受损伤等问题，他们怕惊动上访旁人和当地省公安厅警察？</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">他们还用手捂住我的嘴，还把我的头部按下压打凶残捏住我脖子猛撞头至昏，身体全身暴伤没有及时治伤病，造成后遗症严重，还遭被反复暴殴严刑迫供</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">经村民叙述在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">16</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日早上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点左右突被顺德区容桂街道容里居委主任</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">梁敏英</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">配合佛山市副市长邓伟根（原顺德区容桂街道党委书记）亲自挂帅拉几只警犬带领警力</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多个</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1000</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多辆警车、携带冲锋枪、轻机枪、电棍，盾牌围攻浩劫容里村与进入大西围（原容里村土地名）工地、容里村的道路，假借阻工用莫须有的罪名，按名单拘捕几十个维权村民（当日官方报纸也报道，在顺德看守所也见此报），其中是与政府对话协商的村民代表，这就不了了知，终断了协商之路，使村民无法与政府接触协商，有些村民叙述说他在酒楼身后有人一拳打倒落地便铐了送进拘留所，这恐怖场面容桂地区史无前例，老人家说当年日本鬼子进村也没有他们这么疯狂恐怖（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2017</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">28</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日邓伟根被双规。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2017</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日容里村民舞狮打鼓放炮竹庆祝邓伟根被双规）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，这强权是十足的白征白食的强抢强征权利霸占了。村官梁敏英以权谋利享用着侵吞村民的得益串通容桂公安，街道办，官商勾结等强盗逻辑霸占了容里村民辛苦积聚的庞大财产资源，以权剥夺了容里村民的长期利益脱离了群众，村官梁敏英被容桂街办违法任命容里居委主任</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">16</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年多了使村民得不到原有的生活水平。带来了村民的倒退生活，使老农民捡汽水瓶破纸皮等废品来维持生计，一个小康富裕村试点成一个贫困村</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我自已醒来就问：</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">你们是什么人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">？为什么打我？他们称</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">是白的（白就是警察）你有鈛不收</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。另一接着说：</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">几千名村民都不信访，你偏信访，有钱收就收。没钱收就算呢！现在受苦受难只是你一人，何必这样做自讨苦吃</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”......</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">便车快速地驶入顺德大良街大良派出所里，然我被几个女工作员押入大良街派出所的二楼审讯室里，将我李碧云扣手锁入老虎凳上，当一穿便服人说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李小姐我不想打你的，我要养家活儿，供车供楼加新，我不做别人也做</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。我想说话</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，因脖子被捏抓损伤严重，使声带已发不出声音，因头部被撞击疼痛厉害得昏昏迷迷，我身上双手又青又淤，我写字请求帮我去医院治疗。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">但他们不理会并说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">你签名了就给你睇医生</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">；他们分别对我严刑轮流审讯，轮流逼供、叫我承认指派容里村民</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">郭顺友</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">到容桂街道的兴华派出所声援容边村民维权，因</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">郭顺友</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在容边兴华派出所里掉汽水并，影响派出所正常工作；无人性的李志堃霍炳潮等人多次刑逼民女李碧云签名</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">聚众冲击国家机关罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，我没有签名（一个弱女怎能聚众冲击国家机关罪？），没按李志堃以</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">25</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">聚众冲击国家机关罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的笔录签名，并多次压我身体踢我身体、他们又把我拉到地下另一个黑室里，一直压住我身体逼我签名，因我不按照签名，而被猛踢入枱底等衣服上衣都整烂了，有另一派出所的人说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">继续这样她会死的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，我才不再暴打，把我从枱底拉出，又把我押上二楼的审讯室</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> ……</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">被多次严刑逼供酷刑致残【因头部多次被撞击至昏，严重损伤脑部神经系统，身体多次被猛打踢，脊椎骨</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">v</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">型骨折、腰椎被打折三折、尾椎粉碎性骨折，颈椎</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">、</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">、</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">折被捏弯曲，口腔被扭弯，胆总管暴伤严重（释放在南方医院做手术的）】。当日已打哑了，几个月后才能发出正常声音。已被刑暴到全身伤痕累累了就关押顺德看守所</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">254</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">女仓，深夜我又被张丽周管教、四眼所长，队长等拉出仓，到第一个审讯室由</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个人轮流审讯（一穿制服，其他便服，不出示证件）指着我威胁恐吓我说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">你知道，你已经犯法，派传单，阻碍国家工程，你不签，没问题，随时判你十年八年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，我无法发出音，伸出青紫的手腕，并指我的上衣被扯难了，呀呀呀！她（李碧云）还不服气，不认罪，不签名，把她带回入仓</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因我没按人为认定的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">聚众冲击国家机关罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的笔录签名，又身体五脏六腑痛得喘气困难，都不带我治病，造成伤病留下严重后遗症</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我被当局派容桂副局长李志堃刑警队长霍炳潮等跨市绑架先严刑逼供暴伤严重，造成我身体伤害严重无及时治疗留下后遗症，五脏六俯受伤历害而吐血、胆总管严重受损（出狱了又转到广州南方医院要做微创手术清除淤血的），被刑讯逼供暴打至贤与肝功能严重受损伤连大小便都不能拉出来而休克，因内伤严重得不至及时治疗而后遗症严重（从此李碧云失去了健康身体】从此扭转我的人生的开始。。。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日下午</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点多送我武警监医院。被单一针对构陷我</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">聚众冲击国家机关罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">不成。然后，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2009</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日再李志堃霍炳潮伪造假口供等官室操作。没有任何的医生诊断证明照片，又不做牙齿敏合鉴定，以单方的伪证伪鉴定就是冤案为目的。认定李碧云咬伤李志堃霍炳潮的手腕制作</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">妨碍公务罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">递交到顺德区检查院而逮捕。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">根据宪法规定</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">妨害公务罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">侵害的对象，是依法正在执行职务的国家机关工作人员。阻碍国家机关工作人员不是依法正在进行的执行公务范围的活动。李志堃霍炳潮曾喜顺等</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7-8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个人穿便服开便车跨市到越秀区执行任务是晃子！是打击报复上访人是真的。是司法机关配合腐败顺德容桂街道办书记列海坚，容里居委会主任梁敏英等刻意就是冤枉案子出来，就是千方百计将我的冤枉案子办成</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">铁案</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">杀鸡儆猴</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">为达目的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">了难案</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">镇压容里维权村民，与此往后，凡是容里居委会主任梁敏英卖容里村民的土地建商品谋取私利都重复式单一绑架暴打针对嫁祸李碧云坐狱，来镇压容里村民出来维权</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">日顺德区检查院配合公安李志堃霍炳潮违法制造数据起诉到顺德区人民法院。一个手无缚鸡之力的弱女子，被</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6-7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我从口袋里，拿出早上呕出的瘀血要求鉴定与身体受伤鉴定；</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">’</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">有期</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我用管教身份你不要上诉，早出去医病。走都不能正常走</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。与此送判决书的光头老说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">如上诉，再判你长些时间</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。我没有被威胁与恐吓而退宿，我在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">天内提起上诉，但维持了原判没有开庭一直回避</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因我伤病越来越严重犯病昏迷，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">天（因暴重伤没有及时治而留下日后遣症，虽在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2010</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年期间曾说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">是找人打她（李碧云）是教训佢一下，也不知道他们出手咁重</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我身体稍好转，然践行申冤，分别到区、市、省，国家各级政府、公检法机构及省委投诉、均得不到纠正的机会。举报反被李志堃等民警绑架身体被刑残（称</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">为升官发财养家糊口</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">妨碍公务罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">为贪腐官</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222;
