mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">22</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日早上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点许，我被搬上法院的牢车，由警车开路，押运到顺德黑法院的庭审上，我在庭审中，诉说了被刑暴逼供虐待折磨的事实</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在庭审中，李冰审判长不顾我身体出现严重不适，不得不申请法庭予以延期审理，但是，又经过</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日、</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日开庭审理。两位律师帮我无罪辩护，与此，审判长李冰毫不顾及李碧云极度身体虚弱，无力发言的身体状况。毫不顾及我尚未最后陈述，毫不顾及辩护人的恳切请求，强行宣布闭庭，法院完全剥夺我的陈述权，从而限制我的辩护权，强行将我抬出法庭，强行</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">完成</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">了一审庭审，强行被带回看守所医务室里，因我全身抽蓄发抖，从嘴边一直流口水出来，但我说不出话来，然一个穿制服的监医来了，望了一望我说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">维什么权，第几次入来，死不了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，拉翻入仓。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我又被带回虐待折磨我的顺德看守所的牢龙里，只</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">40</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方注的牢房里，就关押了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">60</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多的嫌疑人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因被暴伤也被虐待折磨身体差不定时昏迷，得不到治疗还指使涉嫌人不友羡招呼我：</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">指使同仓的涉嫌人将我身体分别四个人向不同方向拉，有两人将我左右手不同方向拉，有两人将我左右脚分别拉开，拉啊拉把我身体分别向四个方向拉到我醒来为止；</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在火辣辣的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7-9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月间指使同仓的涉嫌人将我背到医务室的病床上将我手脚锢定锁住，将我身体分别用</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3-4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">张军棉被盖住我身体至嘴边，焗啊焗焗到我全身出汗而咳咳自已醒来；</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">指使同仓的涉嫌人将我身体丢在有水的地方躺下自已醒；</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，指使同仓的涉嫌人将我嘴巴强行撬开塞入不知什么药入嘴巴，使我脸部撕裂痛和头部爆炸疼痛历害而醒（他们受管教医生指令参与做这些违法缺德不人道行为，他们承认为了早日出监等有奖食品）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">所在狱中受尽了多方面的不人道磨酷折磨虐待残体不成人形了</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日下午约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点，被张丽周管教话带我医务室帮我治疗，当同仓的友人扶我走出仓里沿走廊用轮椅推我时，不料未到医务室被容桂街办组织恐怖分子拦住了，却顺德法院审判长李冰冒出来说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李碧云现宣读判决书在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">17</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日作出《（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）佛顺法刑初字第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">577</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号》犯</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">妨碍公务罪免于刑事处罚释放（从</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2013</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日至</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日共</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">434</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">天），当李冰审审判长话音刚落（后按法律时间向佛山中院提起上诉）。我突被顺德区容桂街办容桂民警苏发等十多人按住我手脚捆住，并用全盔笠住头部抬上便车，我被秘密运出顺德看守所弃于容里村的容里书院区域的路边释放（附图）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">第六案，被连锁报复针对连十年之久的住房和店铺都被违法强拆（使李碧云失去栖身之所，断了经济收入）<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年同日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日傍晚我家人和刘律师在容里村的书院路旁寻到我。然后带我回家看到一片悽惨的废渣惨不忍睹，可在那片废墟中，自古就有砸人家屋不能砸锅的说法，锅还破碎的在那放着，眼睁睁看着那片废墟中，自己辛苦建立的住房栖身之所和按宪法搞富业经济收入的店铺的店铺（共</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">864</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方米）被知法违法的容桂街办领导下令强拆变成瓦砾垃圾，其猖狂凶残程度令人难以想象！，唯一栖身之所的住房和经济收入的店铺被无故强拆没有了模样，住房放的财物也被抢劫了，无了住房，无了经济收入，身体又被暴伤残，这惨景泣不出声啊！无法用任何的语言去表达</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我出生于广东省佛山市顺德区容桂街道容里村原村民，我在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2005</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年已自建成的住房和店铺（附图）是合法的私人财产，据《宪法》第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">13</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">条第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">款规定，公民的合法的私有财产不受侵犯受法律保护的，该地是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">70</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年代分配我们一家</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">口人的自留地，按宪法该自留可用来搞富业和建住房的，其部分自留地父母在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">80</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年代建了民宅（占地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">118</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方两层半建筑）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">然后，我在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1995</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年期间我申请在自留地建设住房，当年容里村辛基队的队长梁仲开已签名了，又据顺府办（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2001</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">85</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号文，又据</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1999</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月广东省省委，政府的试点，据《土地管理法》等法律法规总一方案，于我在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2005</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年建住房店铺的，建的期间很多村民也来问下也来帮忙的，但没有来政府有关部门说违建！？但是，我父母在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">80</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年代建的民宅（占地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">118</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平米两层半建筑）的房产证而被工作员失误将姓</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">写错姓</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">梁</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，就父母退回村委一直未更正，在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2002</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年父母都过身了。父母希望子女跟进找有关负责部门更正姓</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的房产证（但至今</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2024</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年了有关部门也不原更正，这块地是肥肉之地啊！）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">....<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（一）容桂街道办只是一个派出机构，其职责是：负责管理、协调与服务，又何来的暴力强拆之权？强拆人还称</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">断李碧云既没有房子住也没有经济钱收入皆我住房与店铺的地理位置不错的（交通方便，中小学，市场，居委会，民警中队，公园等设施就近，在容里村属中心位置的），我的住房和店铺（共</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">864</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方米）位于广东顺德区容桂街道容里村的中心要道在容里利群路</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">39</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号（是父母</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">80</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年代建设的民宅）的民宅以东，以北，以西还在营业的。已近十年之久了一直承租别人做生意的，怎在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">25</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日成了广东佛山市容桂街办官方出公告是违法建筑的？法理天理何在？强拆时我还关押在顺德看守所。也不给予我家人说法！何来冒出一个朱卫国在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月出资建筑的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">？而在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">28</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被滥权违法的佛山市顺德区容桂街道办（书记赖雪晖）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">两违</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">领导侵权与容里居委会村官梁敏英等官室操控下，委派原容桂街容里民警中队队长卢能业（警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">192166</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）带有关组织部门，强行拆房铺强制将抢妹的手机和弟摄像机，把我妹弟打伤强把他们的手机与摄像机的取证内容毁灭的。将我李碧云十年之久的住房店铺（约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">864</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方米）针对选择性粉碎式夷为平地（并声称要断李碧云的栖身之所和经济收入，从此李碧云失去栖身之所与店铺的经济收入）。使我居无定所，然姐妹弟照顾我收留我住，而姐被当局害死家破人亡、弟妻离女散、妹被强拆民宅等株连惨憬迫害。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日我刑释放了，次日第二天家人和朋友就带我到广州慈善医院，中山医院等医院治病出院，住院期间朋友们的帮忙问候关注关爱，在这充心说声谢谢感恩！！！然后</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2015</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年期间就向顺德区人民政府进行行政复议，顺德区人民政府复议作出《行政复议决定书》顺府行复案（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2015</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">66</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号的具体（容桂街办</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">两违</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）具体行政违法行为（如下复议决定书），在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2016</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月下旬收到一审法院行政判决书作出《（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2015</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）佛顺法行初字第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">153</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号》也是违法行政越权和二审《（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2016</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）粤</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">06</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">行终</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">332</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号（如下行政判决书）等行政侵权违法行为的判决并可获得国家赔偿的。根据《中华人民共和国国家赔偿法》</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">确赔合一</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">基本原则，《中共中央关于全面推进依法治国若干重大问题的决定》</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">合力和实效监督原则</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。同时，被申请人擅自拆除、毁损或侵犯应当承担举证不能的不利后果。根据《民法通则》第八十七条规定</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">:"</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">负有连带义务的每个债务人，都负有清偿全部债务的义务</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。同法第一百三十四条第一款第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">五</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">项规定</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">:“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">承担民事责任的方式主要有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">:....(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">五</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">恢复原状</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">;....”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。《物权法》第三十六条规定</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">:“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">造成不动产或者动产毁损的，权利人可以请求修理、重作、更换或者恢复原状</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。《侵权责任法》第十五条第一款第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">五</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">项规定</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">:</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">承担侵权责任的方式主要有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">:"...:(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">五</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">恢复原状</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">:....”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">有权必有责，用权受监督，失职要问责，侵权要赔偿</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，被申请人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容桂街办）赔偿申请人（李碧云）所造成的一切损害依法承担和履行国家赔偿责任。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我向容桂街道办申请行政赔偿义务，但容桂街道办党委书记刘国兴孙春光和容里居委会主任兼村书记梁敏英等说话出尔反尔，不履行法定职责依法赔偿。难道两级法院的判决和顺德政府的决定书在现任容桂街道办领导（（原刘国兴书记现顺德区政协副主席）和容里居委会梁敏英眼里就是一张废纸？不按判决履行赔偿义务单位赔偿给予李碧云，而国家国务院，中纪委和省纪检，省政府，佛山纪检，佛山政府、顺德政府，顺德区纪检不督促不监管执行容桂街办依法合理赔偿（或恢复原状与支付每月出租累计租金款），皆容桂街办（党委书记刘国兴，容里村官梁敏英）不履行赔偿义务职责，而我被针对连锁报复迫害制造事端并株连家人亲姐致死的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（二），我盼着</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">办</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，当局不予</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">办</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">睇病遭千里绑架暴打虚待、被关黑监狱<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我住房和店铺被强拆，而我贏了官司输了钱失去自由！赔偿义务单位容桂街办拖而不办。于李碧云向上级政府与纪委等反映并寻求有关部门解决问题，就是法律赋予公民的一种合法权利的途径。而被容桂街办领导与（容里村官梁敏英）等指派容桂民警杜博添等跨市暴力绑架，旧伤未好添新伤，因我的身体严重虚弱不断发病昏迷，而</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2016</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">28</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日突昏迷地铁上不醒，被送入广州的医院半夜才醒来。医生话无能力帮我治病，然推荐我到上一级医院，于我在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2016</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">30</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日坐飞机到北京找多间医院治伤病。经两个月的寻医生对症治疗，身体好转脱离轮椅了，还在疗程治病</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">却不料，在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2016</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">31</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日旁晚被滥用职权的顺德政府容桂街办派官警跨省千里迢迢到北京搜索追杀一个手无缚鸡之力的弱女李碧云，于李碧云落荒而求生</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">当我由</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">120</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">抬上救护车推出某馆门口时</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">...</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">已惊动军政部，国务院，外交部，朝阳公安，信访局等部门，再被北京朝阳警察借核查李碧云身份而拒归还身份证证件（被违法克扣，而被当局借扣押我身份证（由</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2016</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">31</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日晚至</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2022</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日），剥夺我退休金</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">39</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个月的实事</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">....</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">120</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">救护车驶入了中日友好医院急诊室里</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">次零晨，没有法律依据，被佛山市顺德区政府容桂街办腐败官警在天子的眼皮下肆意妄为得进几十人与京</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">车辆闯进在北京中日友好医院里肆无忌惮将病人李碧云强行用擕拿法扭伤双手，差点右手都被扭折连拿一张</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">A4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">纸都拿不动</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">再强制将民女李碧云拖上京</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">Q</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">商务车（并说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">你跑得哪里？我们一样捉住你</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">是的，保我安全</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，而我不安全，而被暴打被绑），一会儿，京</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">Q</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">商务车驶到一个园子里停车，然我在灯光下看到将一扎扎的人民币递给这帮凶，在腐败黑幕官场的操作下我被顺德政府腐败分子暴力强制从北京中日友好医院里押上车后运送一个黑园再转车</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，与此跟随</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7-8</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">商务车有坐在我身旁的是北京领导人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多亩，但是被抢占了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">Q</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">商务车直驶入容里居委里，已整齐列队排好两队工作员（有容里居委领导，容桂街道领导，容桂民警等人员）拍手欢迎北京领导司机等到达顺德容桂</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">难道这</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7-8</span><span style="color: #222222; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">北京领导和司机被欢迎入了容里居委会里边了，我却被容桂民警把我受伤的李碧云押入警车直驶顺德区容桂街道马岗村的民警中队里停车，然将我押入一楼的密室里，几个人强行把我的衣服不人道强制脱落一丝不挂搜取物件等，把我行李包翻了几次，他们看了包里的东西喜欢就拿了没还</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，然后将我拖拽另一审讯室审讯，又逼供你（李碧云）违法，要我签字同年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">有口难辩护啊！欲加之罪？我没有按照签笔录，被他们不道德用人把我身体</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个，右</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">个），太恐怖完全密不透风，我被刑伤恳求治病而不给治，胸闷呼吸困难跟随换班人出门口吸气，而被恐怖者揪头发猛撞击头部至昏迷</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">等也到顺德公安信访和信访部门反映寻我李碧云，而我姐李仪云被强行绑架打伤了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.......&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; mso-ligatures: none;">人为灾难</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2016</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">但将我的身份证证件强行抢夺。我在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2016</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">日重办身份证证件而当局被拒取。于李碧云报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因我十年之久的住房与经济收入店铺被容桂街办违法强拆了，赢了官司失去自由，赔偿义务单位新官上任的容桂街办党委书记刘国兴（现顺德区政协副主席）、孙春光（现顺德杏坛党委书记）等不作为不赔偿，还层级谎言汇报至国务院己给予李碧云合理赔偿了。不但不将住房店铺恢复原状也不合理赔偿，使我失去栖身之所与店铺出租的经济收入。一波未停一波又起，违法强拆伤人劫财有理，苦主无家可归举报有罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">又被容桂街道官警控制人身自由了，使我们的小康生活返贫了，正因侵吞卖容里村几百亩土地款与高额</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（五）顺德居委选举是黑箱操纵的<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月期间佛山市顺德区容桂街道容里社区第六届选举，居委会的主任，副主任和委员，由本居住地区有选举权的居民选举产生的，应该采取民主的方法，不得强迫命令的，首先容里村官有基层街道办，容桂公安等腐败官警的后盾，继续违法选举连任而容里居委会第六届违法又继续操控了，违反了《村委委会组织法》《选举法》等，操纵了整个容里村人员的投票人数，把指定的投票名单梁敏英</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，张耀令，胡祺昌、潘结峰等四人放在枱面上照名字写票</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，让代写工作员并误道投票员就按照贴在抬上的名单抄写选票名单的（如右下图）。。。。与此同时，当李碧云一弱女到现场投票站入投票场里投票都被数位违法跟着距离</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">50</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">分跟着控制人身体自由（如左下图）李碧云怎有能力做一点错事呢？全体社区人员村官梁敏英将继续控制整个容里村物业土地的一切资源。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（六）冲着李碧云而株连弟李添强家，而姐被侵权害死<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&nbsp; </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李碧云只是普通的手无缚鸡之力的村姑，只是一个实事叙说，为自已的家园被入侵自已的土地和资源被掠夺自已的权益被侵害时，也要坚决地保护自已的家园，有什么错？有什么</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">敌对</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">仇恨宿怨？而顺德区容桂街办多届领导班子部分主要成员串谋容桂街容里居委主任兼村书记梁敏英以职务之便以位欺霸、官商勾结从村民手里的好东西夺过来，为了阻止村民维权，就</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">杀鸡儆猴</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">来镇压村民，一味追打着一弱妇女李碧云咬住打，严重侵犯妇女权益的恶性案件，谁出来维权象李碧云一样</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">招呼</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">对待！为了搞分化家人被顺德区容桂街道领导和容里居委梁敏英用权力冲着弱女李碧云而株连迫害家人，并指派容桂民警杜博添（警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">191031</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）和蔡景新（警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">191019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）等滥权任意妄为多次闯入李添强民宅强行暴力抓李添强关押囚禁在振华派出所一天，容里派出所三次几拾小时，金榜派出所一天，德胜派出出所一天等，多次被殴打晕迷，制造事故用摩托车撞骨折手，报警不处理，连未出生的孩子都株连，让弟媳妇生产时故意制造生育事故差点丢命（后续治疗费二十多万元）</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">贏了官司失去自由，我到医院探望姐都被拦截不准。将车拦截围堵等不好行为，因姐收留我住帮我寻医治病，而被顺德容里居委官梁敏英等指派民警杜博添等官警扰民侵权迫害姐又无故打伤姐，因生活困难又将母亲的股份钱扣押（理由是我李碧云不能提供身份证），而姐的病不能及时治疗而病危了。只在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2017</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日是姐从广州医院病危回到家中的，我李碧云只能到姐家看姐最后一面的。姐侵权被害死了（死于</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15%</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">给予我提留地的留用地和我和家人宅基地分配地</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">。我连续报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18511224177</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号码锁住不能报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">如此不可思议。后我为避开梁敏英迫害而到大良逢沙村妹李彩云家栖身</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">天，这，就是法治？</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; mso-ligatures: none;">号），而容桂街办（党委书记刘国兴，容里村官梁敏英）容桂派出所等组织跨街道违法派兵数拾人分班在妹李彩云家门口筑起帐篷日夜守着监视限制我人身自由，离李碧云</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">分就有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个男人贴身围住，一样不准承坐公交车、滴滴车、长途汽车、地铁等交通公具</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我在妹的菜地摘菜一样前后左右守着，这四至五班人，聘请的雇佣兵受指令了，做泯灭良知的寻衅滋事，若有时只是我一个人的，他们为寻衅滋事，我被下三流阴招手段殴打，拦截，围截，推伤害我李碧云身体为泄愤工具，而报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的一样不理会，五史书上，所谓的坏人，也不一定是坏人，所谓的好人，啊啊！也未必就是为老百姓办实事的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">..... &nbsp;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我李碧云与大良街道办领导副书记叶善楷无怨无仇。而被大良街办、大良街派出所配合容桂街办书记刘国兴容里村官梁敏英、容桂公安等利用职权串谋策划人为制造灾难</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">并将李碧云和弟打入泥浆里</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">时许要去大良人民医院看病，公交车站与公交车都有安装电子设备监控录像的。我在大良街道逢沙会龙站（有监控视频下）承坐</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">307</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">路公交车去，而被容桂街道掌权官派出所謂工作员拦住李碧云乘坐公交车，还用专车粤</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">X96096</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，粤</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">X96090</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">本田车拦截粤</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">X33315</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号牌的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">307</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公交车行驶的。李碧云随即报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，同时也当值司机也报警，因我被当局派的人阻止我承坐公交车，二又被当局派的人推拽我身体昏昏迷迷。三我身体又虚弱，四我身体顶不住</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月天的猛烈酷炎毒热的天气，虽一好心村民给了我一支水喝，而我中暑昏倒公交车边。后来大良派出所德胜民警中队出警，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">307</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的公交司机也向德胜民警中队的民警说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">是有多名男子阻止一名女子（草民李碧云）上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">307</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号公交车，而造成公交车不及时离开的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。出警民警也进行拍摄取证，将已中暑的李碧云扶到路边树靠着，没事休息下。并说李小姐你去睇病坐他们的专车更方便，说完后民警也离去，村民也一一散开。剩下</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9-10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个顺德恐怖分子守着我李碧云昏昏迷迷在路边树靠着。经逢沙村民告知我妹发生的事故，然妹傍晚约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点来到逢沙会龙站，见我昏昏迷迷依靠在会龙站的树旁上，我每日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">小时被地方官违法监控人身自由，容桂街办派的工作人还在守着的，然妹抽我上电动车载我回家的。本以为事情画上了句号了，岂知事态后进一步权力手段的连锁迫害。同日晚上约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点有一群人自称公安大声说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">要传呼李碧云，开门跟我们到德胜派出所。因我中</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">署</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">热，我喝了去署的凉药，正躺在床上。而被大声叫嚣的声音叫醒了。我妹要求他们把工作证和传呼证给我们看看，为什事传呼我李碧云？你李碧云阻止公交车行驶。我承坐公交车被拦截拖拽至昏倒，为何成了拦阻公交车？我一个弱女子在监控下有胆骨阻止公交车行驶？</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">但这群人一直不给传呼证和任何工作证，在妹民宅四周转了几转后，这些人无声走了。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（二）借传呼爆民宅闯民灾，绑架伤人洗劫民财</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">14</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">51</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">分一村民至电妹李彩云到她家，刚巧我妹李彩云</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222;
