font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">分被支开家。突然李彩云细儿子说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">三姨楼下来很多土匪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。我（李碧云）正蹲厕所被惊吓而按花洒把衣服弄湿了。容桂民警蔡景新</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">14</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">58</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">分（监控视频显示）带几十个民警到达李彩云家门口，容桂在场民警蔡景新说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">传唤你李碧云关于昨日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日阻碍公交车一事</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。我（李碧云）说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">大良逢沙村会龙站是属大良街道派出所处理的事，传呼我用不用带这么多人来，又这么多车，你蔡景新是容桂民警的；若传呼我属大良派出所？住宅是我妹李彩云的，私人住宅不得随意侵入私人财产的场所不受侵犯的，让我妹回家我跟你们走一趟，请你们给我传呼证法律文书和你们的工作证看。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我至电妹李彩云回来，我坐在一楼梯级的门口等我妹回来时候。容桂公安副局蔡景新完全没有紧迫情和必要情派上特警组进行破门冲入民宅传呼我，一面李碧云被蔡景新指挥用塑料带强反扭我双手至我右手扭伤，双脚用塑带扣死，强行数人拖拽我上面包车丢下，那么被捆绑拖拽的暴力法野蛮执法过程为何不记录？另一面蔡景新带的几十个穿着制服冲上二、三楼地毯式掠夺财物和搜他们违法证据；传唤李碧云是幌子，是入民宅抢财物是真的。为何把李彩云女儿的电脑，李碧云的电脑，李碧云的已经签证护照抢夺，与李碧云的案件的复议，申诉，诉讼证据材料和硬盘</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">U</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">盘，也盗走的；我们的几台手机，连利是钱</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">元至</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">100</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">元都盗走，电视机的储存卡也劫走，我妹李彩云的儿子惊慌过度关了房门都被土匪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">民警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">撬烂房门强行抢走李彩云儿子玩游戏的苹果电脑，，令到我妹儿子十天也不敢出门口；同时把我妹民宅案有关政府信息公开文件和顺德法院复印文件一系列资料被抢劫了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">家中楼层上上下下都被一一搜索、抢的抢、偷的偷损坏严重，报</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，顺德公安机关不出警不立案。面对这样来势汹汹的黑恶势力打着共产党旗号的顺德政府官的顺德容桂派出所和德胜派出所民警强行爆李彩云家门冲入民宅洗劫财物后，还荒谬毫无道理可言，力求目的达到横行霸道强迫李彩云要签</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">搜查令</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。该民警人警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">191019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">嚣张气焰我们不怕你们投诉，你们投诉都多了，你们有用吗？谁给这民警的权力凌驾于法律之上？事实报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">顺德公安不予立案侦察！！！难道穿警服故意随之任意爆门冲入民宅洗劫财物？？难道顺德区容桂街道办独立办案变成</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">独立王国</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">？</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">将我李碧云强行用塑带反扣手，右手被民警警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">191019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">爪擒捏伤右手手指脱臼与双脚被绑架到大良街德胜民警中队里的审讯室</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，将我身体反锁在老虎凳上，不友善的多时审讯</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">后来，我妹李彩云和弟李添强到德胜中队了解事件，德胜中队民警说不知道，这是容桂公安的事件。他们借德胜中队办理。既然是为公交车事情又不是大良德胜中队办理。致电容桂街道领导。并向他说明公交车不是李碧云阻拦的。是跟随的政府官员不准李碧云到看病的，也不用公车车李碧云去，才李碧云搭公交车车看病的。容桂领导致电说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">了解问题后才回复</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。在不友善的审讯中，①当晚</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点左右释放李碧云回家了，过几天才把我们的电脑，手机，苹果手提还回。但还有电脑，手机共三台未还。我李碧云的护照未归还，首饰钱财未还。这明显是容桂公安陷害报复我李碧云要求解决多年被软禁和强拆我们的房屋未赔偿的问题</span><span style="color: #222222; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">本以为事情到此画上一个句号的，岂料事态的用一切权力手段的迫害发展。何乎相隔</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">米，平均公园大约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">100</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）地理位置好，在华侨城就近的地铁口。只是顺德政府官以权收购而纳入征收我妹李彩云民宅地，根据</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&lt;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">物权法</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&gt;</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">证内与证外都有合法补偿费的，收购或征收李彩云房屋不要降低李彩云原有生活，要保障日后生活水平，我妹李彩云经过三番五次与顺德官方拆迁部门的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">‘</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">大良街办拆迁叶主任、逢沙村潘主任、</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">逢沙村收购项目拆迁办李主任和综治办工作员的协商。因我国房屋征地拆迁中</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">先补偿后搬迁</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">"</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">已法律规定的。在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月底叶善楷大良街副书记组织拆迁部门与妹李彩云协商达成协议了，于下星期双方签订征收协议书的</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">却不料，一方面大良街办书记叶善楷和拆迁办等负责人与妹达成征收协议了，却突袭搅</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">人为灾难</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日上午约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点大良街办（党委副书记叶善楷、逢沙村拆迁主任李志宗，潘礼华指挥现场）配合容桂街办（党委书记刘国兴，容里村官梁敏英，容桂公安局长汪刚副局长蔡景新）等</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">利</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">字当头作崇，在利益政绩的驱动下，一呼百应非法聚集</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">300</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多持械蒙面人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">两头堵</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">式势如破竹，一边</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多持械蒙面人拿铁叉、铁棒、铁网的海盗行为爆开民宅大门闯入李彩云民宅，冲上二楼强把我妹按住，将妹手中一岁的孙子抢走，再将我妹被绑架押上面包车，将她困住在顺德区大良殡仪馆旁的巷口里几天。将李彩云民宅</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">、</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">、</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">层的财物品和李碧云李添强的财物电脑证件私自强行洗劫一空。故意暴伤人、砸、抢、劣、等违法偷拆李彩云民宅夷为平地了，使李彩云无家可归。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">另一边见李彩云家人就持械追打，我李碧云与弟李添强与李添强三岁女儿距离妹李彩云的住宅约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">100</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">米正在摘菜的，旁边也围着数个监控我人身自由的政府聘请的雇佣兵，与此突几十个蒙面人拿着铁叉铁棒铁网疯狂地凶残朝着我（李碧云）与弟李添强追打并</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">高喊按住佢</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的气焰嚎叫，我们惊恐逃离，都将我（李碧云）按入泥泞里至昏右手骨折等身体胸口腰椎暴伤，窒息昏迷差点掉命等多次软组织受伤，然将全身泥浆的李碧云拉上来，然将我带离案发现场押上面包车，我左右后被作案人按着，面包车一直驶向容桂街道办事处里停下，一会儿，受指示把我满身泥浆的李碧云押运到容里村在弟民宅公路边丢下，还将李碧云随身包里的几百元人民币与手机【三星</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">NO3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（手机号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18511224177</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">）三星</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">NO5,</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">华为，银行卡等被抢劫了】至今还未归还。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">而李添强也被拿武器铁棒、铁叉、铁网戴口罩数拾人追打着，凶残用铁叉叉住李添强身体头部按入泥泞里猛压打直窒息了，才把满头满身泥浆昏迷的李添强从泥泞里拉上来，然后将其抬进</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">120</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">救护车，从大良街逢沙村永安东路</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号民宅旁押运到容桂街道办事处</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">→</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">然又</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">120</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">押运到容桂派出所里</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">→</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">又继续押到新地民警中队</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">→</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">然到容里民警中队</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">被打伤的李添强没有送进医院治疗，李添强在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">120</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">车上一直恳求它们带他到医院治疗，以伤为重，先治疗先，但不理会。只是用</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">120</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">救护车运载李添强到处跑的，不准李添强到案发现场。再后在容桂街道容里民警中队里迫李添强用水把头部睑上眼睛身上的泥泞冲干净后，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点才释放李添强回家。但弟身上的手机和人民币证件也被抢不归还。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">惨无人道的人为灾难现场有大良街办副书记叶善楷，逢沙村拆迁主任李志宗，潘礼华指挥现场等，顺德公安</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">民警在那瞧着，顺德区行政执法队等人员在场</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，与串谋顺德区容桂街道书记刘国兴容里村官梁敏英等组织</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">300</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多蒙脸人极度恶劣人为设计</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">两头堵</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">式没有任何人去制止？对于此蛮横暴力，就算是强拆难道就拿武器，指向目标追打人按入泥泞里窒息骨折了等不同程度受伤？强拆故意伤人抢劫民财绑架事件；一边被</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">200</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多人戴口罩拿武器强悍男人，以执法名义，却强盗山贼海盗行为，气焰嚣张强拆民宅，国家公务蛮横凶残无理，大声嚎叫，我是法律，警察在场不理</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">...</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">触目惊心的画面，妹被绑架，妹家财劫空和李碧云，李添强，李添强女儿被抢夺的钱财物品，李碧云十年签证护照被盗走等证件，我们身体的故意伤害未赔偿，妹民宅变成灰尽，消灭在空气中</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在打黑除恶的今天，习近平主席呼喊依法治国，依法行政。在我国房屋征地拆迁中</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">先补偿后搬迁</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">"</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">已法律规定的。并在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月底叶善楷大良街副书记组织拆迁部门与妹李彩云协商达成协议了，而被政府公职刘国兴一声下令</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">以李彩云收留李碧云住才袭击强拆</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，这是什么法理？强制拆迁就可以暴残解决的话那么现在提倡的法制社会就是废话，行政执法难道真的没有人管？？？所谓执法人员？？所谓的顺德政府人员，所谓的人民的顺德民警？他们用手中的权利就可以肆无忌惮的进行任何凶残行为，这就是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">合法</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">？这幕后的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">保护伞</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">是谁？</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">当晚释放后李彩云女儿梁某仪、李添强，李碧云才有几会报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">等部门，说明以上案发时间地址案情与提供打人证据，希望公安作主，而顺德公安一声说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">拆迁属政府的，我们公安无权管</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，就变成</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">证据不足不予立案</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">了呢？</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">以李彩云收留李碧云住，李彩云民宅才下令被强拆的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。下令强拆的是新任顺德区长（后来才知是刘国兴）就滥用职权聚众数百人，无法无天持械破门、抢夺民财，绑架伤人、毁灭证据等强拆民宅的？皆</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我李碧云住房店铺（共</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">864</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">平方）在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2014</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">28</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被容桂街办强拆的。根据《宪法》第六十八条，行政机关或者行政机关工作人员作出的具体行政行为侵犯公民、法人或者其他组织的合法权益造成损害的，由该行政机关负责赔偿的，而新官上任容桂街办（党委书记刘国兴）不履行职责不赔偿，又不原恢复原状，使我无栖身之所。正因侵吞卖容里村几百亩土地款与高额</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">维稳费</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的驱动下发挥到极至一一</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">无所不能</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，还滥权用人为障碍聘请数</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">雇佣兵监控剥夺我人身自由权和医疗权等，姐（李仪云）收留我（李碧云）一年多就被容桂街办刘国兴与容里居委梁敏英侵权害死了（死于</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2017</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日）；再妹收留我住一年多了，李彩云民宅就下令被强拆的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“...</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">人为制造</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">两头堵</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">式串谋织织故意伤人劫财绑架等谋夺李彩云私人财产、扩大违法行为，制造大量违法事情、制造社会不和谐，以权掩饰其滥用职权罪，非法侵入住宅罪，抢夺居民财产罪，绑架罪，侵犯通信自由罪，故意伤害罪，寻衅滋事罪，毁灭证据罪等，而顺德公安又不予依法立案侦查，根据《公安机关办理行政案件程序规定》指出，公民报案，公安机关要及时受理并制作受案登记表，及时调查处理并受案回执单交与报案与报案人、立案侦查的、公安是保护百姓的合法财产人身安全不受侵害。同时也给省公安厅、检查院、顺德公安局、德胜中队、大良派出所等各部门申请重建家园和保护一家人身财产安全，却未有回复</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（四）这，就是法治？强拆民宅不赔偿不立案，一家五人被行拘</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">天处罚</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">25</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">农历</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">16</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日晚上在废虚地追月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">把李彩云，李添强、梁巧儿夫妻带走。李添强也是在用手机取证，没闹没骂，而被警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">190520</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">朝李添强滕盖狠毒踢了几下，造成弟李添强双脚站不起来。李添强疼痛辛苦头晕呕吐昏倒，李添强一直恳求帮李添强去治病，但没有带李添强去治病、李碧云坐在地下用手机拍摄现场，也被几个民警把李碧云一推一拉强行推上警车造成身体又不好</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">…</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李碧云被强行押到顺德区公安局大良分局的大室里。民警将李彩云，与李彩云女儿夫妇与李添强的身上手机财物强取走，随即李碧云手机财物也强取走</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我们问看管的，你们大良公安用什么理由关押我们这里。看守人说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我们不知道</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，问容桂街道的领导。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">‘</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">是你们大良街办领导指令的大良公安（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">190520</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">、</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">191424</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的警号）无故捉我们到这里的。为什你们取我们的财物未给清单我们？</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">’</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">看守人说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">大良派出所借地方给容桂街办用。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点前你们的物品给你们可以回家，不给去看守所。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">突然，关押门被打开了，我妹的前夫也被捉来了，他说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我在住的地方被捉的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”........<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-ligatures: none;">人穿便服的人进关押室，我发现很面善</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，我妹没有按他们写好的笔录签名，而被强按上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">市长热线，我（李碧云）的身份证被容桂街道无故扣押</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年有多了，请人道主义，以人为本把身份证归还我，同时，让我办理收养老金手续款，但容桂街办人社保局没有依法帮我办理收养老金手续款（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2022</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月份才办理，而违法剥夺我</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial;
