mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">时我们从容桂街道容里利群路</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">39</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号弟家出门到广州铁路运输法院时。而在家门口已被顺德区容桂街办聘请的雇佣兵在门口拦截不准去广州，只能在顺德区人民法院（顺德村民的黑法院。）诉讼其他地方不能去。于报警</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">出警，经说明理由就让我们走。当我们快到容奇大桥时被跟随的公安用专车突然在后面行驶到前面差点碰到撞车了，跟随公安说。（老板叫你们到容里居委会协商，你们到法院诉讼的事</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，当时我们有公安车特警车和容桂街办聘请的雇佣兵</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">小时监控李碧云的人跟随一起到容里居委会直到我进入容里居委会，公安车特警车才离开，容里居委会跟随的政府人员在门口看守，我们与容里居委会领导街办领导和律师协商不成，下午再谈，我们就回家了。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">当日下午约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点半点再到容里居委会不见领导又叫我们到容桂街道维稳办协商，这样一来二去同意也不能到广州了。我妹和我（李碧云）只好坐公交车去广州，上公交车被跟随的公安拉下车了。不准搭公交车。我李碧云被拉到昏迷，我自已醒来后，公安车和特警车也到场，我妹与公安理论一边扶着我（李碧云）向大良那头走上容奇大桥，过容奇大桥到大良那头桥脚。政府官员叫我们不要走老板有话和你们协商的，我们停下那刻公安车上的人跳下</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8-9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个便衣把我李碧云的电话抢走，我妹打</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">110</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">求助大约当日四点左右，和追这个抢我手机的便衣追不到，我们打完电话走向顺德大良嘉信那头。走到史努比公园旁的路边时（就是顺德区大良街道南霞的红绿灯的人行路）。公安车、特警车、有面包车、有两辆本田街办专车粤</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">X96090</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">与粤</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">X96096</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，当容桂街办书记一声指令</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">捉住佢</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">一呼百应各车上人一拥而上把我们包围起来，恐怕给</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">过绿灯的人们</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">看到我（李碧云）和妹。我还大声喊不要打我了，但我绑架后到容里民警中队更加用刑歹毒了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">!</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我妹被四个大汉拉上面包车</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">( </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">二</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">有罪推定</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">被残酷逼供，身体被数人架起歹毒脊椎暴拆</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我（李碧云）被四男人拉上粤</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">X96090</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">街办车直驶入容里新地民警中队里，然把我随身带的诉讼资料证据钱财、家门锁匙银行卡等全部抢走，等被</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">190666</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">拉到什么车都不知。殊不料拉我入室，几个人强把我衣服脱掉凌辱性搜身</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">为何这样凌辱搜身，明显你们是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">心中贼</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。你收声好过些</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我被拉入审讯室</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，把我抽上老虎凳上，双手被锢定锁住，双脚分别被插入已水泥填的脚洞里，动弹不得。分别室里有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个守住，我多次请求我要小便，但他们不理会，大小便是人生理正常反映的，在监控下小便拉出来了，使异味散发出来，他们轮了几班了，连大良街办的德胜民警也来了守，我要求食饭，但他们不给我</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">过了一段时间，有两个来民警审讯问</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李碧云</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">係年三十晚）你到容桂花市做什么？，我答</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我每日都有街办派的所谓工作员</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">小时违法监视控制我人身自由，象铁桶一样围着我，我报警都不计其数了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“......</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我要食饭，饮水。但要领导批准的，一会儿，拿了一小汤面给我，我食了一些，突然我肚痛得很历害，头疼脑胀得历害而昏倒了，自已醒来裤了更湿了，我问</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">这些面汤放什么有损害人身体的东西？</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">食了我昏了，我眼睛打不开，肚子又很痛，头痛得历害</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。一女自说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我们都食这些的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，言行出卖了他们犯下罪行？我恳求带我去医院治病，并说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我眼睛很痛打不开，肚子又很痛，一民警说你做完笔录就带你睇医生，他们已制好的笔录叫我签，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我说睇不到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，然一审讯人说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我读出来</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">原来我被嫁祸秘密盗摊主的洗水盆槽</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在年三十晚开放式的迎春花市</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">开放式的迎春花市，人山人海，车辆络绎不绝；</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我被监视控制人身自由并且离我</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">50</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">分至</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">100</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">分就有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7-8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">人守着我（同时，我不是齐天大胜孙悟空，我们不能飞天遁地，不会变分身术，眼皮下盯住怎敢做一点错事</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我右手</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">18</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被暴骨折两度等重伤，怎能拿这庞大洗水盆槽？不同的人声对我轮流审讯，轮流逼供。并将我（李碧云）身体用人顶住架起架住身体时，求他们高抬贵手，但这些人阴毒阴招用拳头在我（李碧云）身体背后锤脊椎骨折等受伤，卡的一声痛得当场吐血至昏等残酷的严刑逼供</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">把我妹车到容奇大桥的雁龙酒店门口停下约</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">20</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">分钟，然后面包车驶入容里新地民警中队里。然把妹随身带的诉讼资料证据钱财等全部抢走，凌辱色搜身，即说传唤为何把我们的东西上上下下里里外外一点不漏。恐怕肚里都搜出来。我妹说要去小便，也不给，我妹无法忍受失禁穿着湿淋淋的内裤。气味难闻，几天几夜。被关进顺德看守所都是逼我妹签强拆妹房屋的不合理的赔偿款的。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">与此同时，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">25</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日晚</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">22</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">时李添强被蔡景新等领导以权压法派出公安</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">握枪屠宅</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">破门而入</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李添强住宅、绑架李添强</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">岁女儿，贼警还屠劫将李添强宅内三层楼和园地，杂物房全部喜欢的财物（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">台联想笔记本，多功能打印机，破盘、</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">U</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">盘，电子监控，他们的违法证据）等钱财物屠劫一空、将李添强暴力殴打强暴抓押到容桂新地民警中队里逼供，恐吓，威胁盗窃年三十晚摊主的物品</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">同年，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月份有一个公安说他是佛山市公安局民警，警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">190907</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，姓冯名超。容桂公安也叫他超哥一共提审了妹七天，都是提审关于妹民宅被强拆房屋赔偿的问题和关于我（李碧云）维权十年给妹三个方案，还要以后不要理李碧云，最好是断绝关系，并且给政府有一个下台的机会，这样大家的事情才能完善，我按政府官员的要求签名，这样能要回你自己的合法赔偿，李碧云的问题也能解决，也对我们日后生活也好，我妹在反对又无奈下按他们的笔录签名。后来有拆迁工作人员来还是比原来少，每次来看守所协商赔偿的人都不同，他们都说，之前你们怎样协商我不知怎样。永远就只做一个样板。在看守所看到，顺德公安办案的黑暗，在看守所用钱的规则，维权群众在看守所的危害。退一万步来，不管我三姐弟和政府人员一起叫搬的行为，是否有错，顺德区政府官员也不能用私刑，对我三姐弟，我们在看守所被逼害，凌辱，体罚，殴打，不给勺子吃饭</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">（三），以</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">盗窃罪名</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">被官商伪证推定，被酷刑虐待迫供</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因为我三姐弟坚持</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">民告官</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">而被绑架后，被残酷逼供，我（李碧云）被用刑提审几日满身臭尿难闻，给食有毒的汤面而眼睛睁不开、肚子又痛、被刑暴折脊椎痛而昏倒吐血等伤害没有送我医院，而被押入顺德看守所女仓，次</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">28</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日零晨</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点多头疼得历害又呕血出来，仓里的人帮按玲，但医生不理我。在早上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点许我因肚痛头痛得历害而昏倒在床板上，我醒来身体躺在湿辘辘的地下。我问</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我昏倒在床上，为什把我李碧云抽在这湿的地下有人回答</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我们是按照医生管教做的，你快醒来，因管教开仓报数，你不能一人留在室内，所我们值班员抬你在这地下</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。监规标明有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">健康权，人体权，生命权</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的。为何这样虐待要人命？<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">同年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日我双手被锁住，然被保安用轮椅推我到审讯室，再把我抽到铁凳上，由两穿制服的人来提审我，只闪一闪工作证说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李碧云摊主严毅华在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">。李碧云你又入来，你今第几次入来？今次衰什么关入来？然医生说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。当他们扶起我时，她裤子湿了，以后不要带入这</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">,,,,</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">皆我一直没有按照当局的制作笔录签名，在仓里被有心人指定仓里人故意刁难我，</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"> </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因身体不好昏倒了将我抽落湿气重的地下让我快醒来（他们说医生管教叫的），甚至被整股到昏倒室内水池里</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">后在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2019</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我说</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">：</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">发生地是大良街道逢沙村会龙站发生的公交车被阻拦事件。如须要传呼也是大良街德胜中队的民警处理的，为何会是容桂民警呢？要点一，当日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的公交司机也向德胜出警民警说</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">307</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。出警民警也进行拍摄取证，并且德胜民警将我中暑的李碧云扶在树边休息。才离开的。要点二，当日</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被容桂民警蔡景新等强行破门带我到德胜中队审问了，经妹与弟了解事件，是容桂街的事情，德胜中队借容桂公安办理。既然是为公交车事情属大良街道的区域，又不是大良德胜中队办理？要点三，传唤李碧云是为会龙站公交车被阻拦问题。没有任何法律文书，为何把我妹女儿的电脑，我李碧云的电脑，签证十年护照，我们的几台手机等盗掠，也撬烂房门强行抢走妹儿子玩游戏的苹果电脑。但我们电脑和手机里面的资料公安违法证据被除掉了，还有多台手机，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">u</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">盘，硬盘，有关公安违证据在公安那里？关健要点四，我李碧云只是一个普通弱女子，只当年参加集体土地维权，而一直针对迫害被视眼中钉，单一被你当地政府</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">小时监控控制人身自由的对象，离我</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">50</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公分至</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">100</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公分的距离，又不准坐任何交通公具（公交车也不准），只准姐妹弟电动么托车，政府官员</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">小时视觉微信对接，与此，煤气油从何店购买呢</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">? </span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">只是</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">欲加之罪，何患无词。要点五，问题当晚</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日晚我妹弟与容桂街办领导等组织双方进行调解成功了，当晚</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点已释放我李碧云回家了。并且，国家主席习近平在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2018</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月份已在各部门成立调解部门的，调解成功是有法律效力的。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">行驶行为的涉嫌，也没有妨碍公务罪名行为的涉嫌。为何时隔</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">个多后，当李碧云和妹到广州铁路法院立案的，就从何而来我妨碍公务罪呢？这摆明滥权针对打击迫害信访人与诉讼人就是嫁祸冤案子的罪名</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">民告官</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的原告反被当局构陷罪名，被贪婪的司法部门腐败分子徇私枉法，利益驱使配合顺德容桂街办书记刘国兴容里村书记梁敏英蔡景新又将手无缚鸡之力的李碧云以</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">敌对</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">残酷手段刑暴瘫痪了，并在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">容里村村民居住一带宣传，一传十，十传百</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">.....</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">谁出来维权就象李碧云一样</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">招呼</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">对待</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。达到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">杀鸡儆猴</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的目的。一切宣传工具都被用来镇压容里村民，受恐慌恐惧的村民受到了影响的，目的是容里村民不敢站出来依法维权投诉了，目标实施资讯垄断了土地资源，又控制了容里村民经济的一切资源了。被蔡景新等官室操作伪证，假证人重读</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">妨碍公务罪</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">转到顺德区检查院而逮捕。但是涉及我们行政诉讼的举报问题和我李碧云被刑残的问题只字不提。而被涉贪污受贿的检查官潘耿凭一人的违法侦查违背良心起诉到顺德区人民法院。违背了自然、不符合情理、逻辑错误、前后矛盾伪造谎言</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">‘</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">与顺德容桂公安串谋的事实；是故意报复陷害被告李碧云、李添强、李彩云</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">......<o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">六）权谋获利朋党的腐败链被伪证枉法冤判</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">妨碍公务罪和盗窃罪</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">8</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">29</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">15</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日在顺德黑法院的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">天审理过程中，我们三被告都是用秘密通道押入法庭的，李碧云、李添强、李彩云诉被拦截抓捕的违法经过，和真实性，关联性，合法法的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">质证、反驳</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公诉机关潘耿官商勾结插桩嫁祸的违法指控</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">……</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">公安违法立案，证人证言做假证，违法侦查，全部言辞证据虚假档主陈述，鉴定意见价格造假等</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">...</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因在听庭与庭审中驳斥公诉潘耿的违法指控，被审判长寥冰寒时时拦截，并要求传唤，所谓受害人，证人，办案人等出庭作证。但审判长寥冰寒不采取，而被虐待不给水喝，不准去小便，使李碧云在庭审中失禁拉尿等，不给饭食，就执法警吃剩丢垃圾桶的剩饭，不给水喝，饮龙头水都不给，伤瘫李碧云被虐待昏倒推到冷气机直吹至醒，监控下为什公诉人潘耿在庭上坐在书记员位置操作？<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因李碧云被违法抓后被公安等严刑逼供暴骨折内伤被中风等残废、大小便不能正常自理，在庭审中向审判长控诉公安严刑逼供致残和申请做伤情鉴定，但寥冰寒等不采取并制止；皆李添强也在庭上控告当局被公安蔡景新等公安握枪屠宅</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">破门而入李添强住宅，任意把李碧云、李添强在住宅一、二、三楼财物和地方官违法证据（电脑，打印机，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">U</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">盘，硬盘、李碧云护照，李碧云多宗冤案的一审、二审，驳回书等诉讼文书和违法抢掠土地证据等地毯式打击迫害的违法行屠洗掠夺财物）（如下图），绑架李添强</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">岁女儿，掠夺民所有民财证据，家里监控全部损坏</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">…..</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">而被阴招虐待当场昏倒。。。。。和律师的质证无罪辩护。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">至于严毅华报案陈述、</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">26</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号档主冯典文、顾育铭、冯永建的陈述，周文龙报案陈述是子虚乌有、一面之词、不足以采信。前后矛盾。官商（摊主）操控、搞</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">一言堂</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">凭空伪证造假、公安机关所作笔录不属实是嫁祸陷害。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">侦查人员在侦查终后补写现场勘验笔录，是存在去伪存真的问题。这证明公安有意插赃嫁祸的伪证。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">涉案不锈钢洗水盘（槽）的认定测算错误，导致价格认定结论真实性存欸，该《价格认定结论书》不得作为定案的根据。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">申诉人及其辨护人在诉讼过程中根据事实和法律对指控的内容进行申述、辩解、反驳、质证控诉。《中华人民共和国<u>刑事诉讼法</u>》第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">55</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">条：</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">对一切案件的处理都要重证据，重调查研究，不轻信口供。不能认定申诉人李碧云（和申诉人李添强、李彩云）有盗窃罪。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">李碧云没有阻拦公交车。李彩云家</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">火水</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">煤油从何而来？李碧云身上衣服有火水就是公安淋的，是蓄意谋财害命。就有意把</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">火水</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">淋到李彩云住宅门口满地。二是李碧云三姐弟</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">民告官</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的原告反被当局构陷盗窃罪名，与此同时，妨害公务罪侵害的对象，是依法正在执行职务的国家机关工作人员。阻碍国家机关工作人员不是依法正在进行的执行公务范围的活动，不构成妨害公务罪。被司法部门腐败分子徇私枉法，利益驱使配合顺德容桂街办书记刘国兴容里村书记梁敏英蔡景新将手无缚鸡之力的李碧云以</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">敌对</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">残酷刑暴瘫痪了。达到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">杀鸡儆猴</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">的目的。受恐慌恐惧的容里村民受到了影响的，目标实施控制容里村民经济垄断了土地一切资源了。是容桂民警卖力都为升官发财，这次卖容里中学旁的几百亩集体土地建</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">东湖学府等建商品楼，又是很大的财源。这拍卖土地款鼓了容里居委村官梁敏英和容桂街道办领导刘国兴，容桂公安等组织领导的</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">口袋里</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，又是容桂公安为村霸梁敏英制造一个妨碍公务罪，造就村官梁敏英卖地，一分钱不分给村民，恐吓村民不要维权，如有维权后果就像我们一样，使村民不敢向有关部门举报。顺德区公检法欺负我李碧云和家人不是第一次。随便撬门拉我李碧云坐牢和殴打，都是容里居委会村官梁敏英卖地的，正因每次捉李碧云坐牢都是梁敏英卖容里村民集体土地的时刻。顺德区政府与属下有关部门故意处处人为为难李碧云和家属，故意找我们麻烦，刁难我们，李碧云与家属向国家有法律法规的部门来维护自身的安全和生命财产错在哪里？做官的为自己政绩利益找李碧云刁难与制造麻烦，利用手里的权利暴打刁难李碧云。李碧云的生命如猴子来玩。软禁、殴打、虐待、凌辱、欺压并抢李碧云的自由权、生命权、健康权、人权。李碧云不存在妨碍公务罪与李碧云妹弟盗窃罪是违法执行公务的行为。就是枉法枉判的。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">过了几天，我和弟被法院工作员指令狱警被锁手锁脚禁锢老虎凳上只听他们读笔录，为什不准看庭审笔录？又不准签字？明知三被告是无辜的啊，明知这个案子三被告都在喊冤啊。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2020</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">1</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">21</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被顺德黑法院审判长寥冰寒配合公检制造了</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">39</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">页长的嫁祸编读判决书《刑事判决书》（</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2019</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">灯下黑</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">佛山中院维持原判。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-ligatures: none;">李碧云被顺德官商勾结的腐败公安残酷刑逼成伤瘫残废等（因自已不能起床，不能自已躺下睡，不能自已正常大小便等中风内伤瘫等）但得不到有效治病。经腐蚀官徇私枉法，又经现场咬</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">耳朵</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">说话，在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2020</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">9</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">5</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日抬到五监区二楼</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号床监舍（一车间）至</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2022</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日刑满释放</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">...</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">监狱是国家政府监管机关，监狱警察是保护服刑人员人身生命安全的，但伤瘫残废李碧云在服刑期间也受尽非人性迫害，为何被五监区警官黄娟</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4455551)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">等监警违良心滥权指使服刑人员非人性多次故意虐待暴打残废李碧云至昏迷</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因头部多次被撞击，身体多次突踢撞腰椎折等酷吏折磨致</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">“</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">瞎哑瘸的废人</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">”</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">，在俾人抽着我双手从三楼走榔拖着我身体一级级拖拽落梯级一楼操场地下，还有</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">700</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">多人服刑人员眼睁睁看着这一幕幕不道德虐待凌辱耻辱的场景</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2020</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">11</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">27</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日寒冬腊月晚上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">10</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点多，残废李碧云睡在被窝里，在狱警的带领下被服刑人员抽起身，由四个人分别抽手抽脚抬到三楼的小厅中，并把我虚弱的身体卷起单上衣，齐丢在寒冬腊月晚上的冷硬地板上，使我身体冷至全身抽畜，口水鼻涕眼泪齐涌出来后，再</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">人分别揪手揪脚的，但左边抽手的服刑人李家玲将我左入扭伤韧带，左手的手指瘀肿至右手指一分二，嘴都弯了，口水鼻涕眼泪齐涌出来更严重，后用轮椅推我监医室，因我身体被折磨虐待说话都不清晰了，医生说我不配合，就不理了</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">第</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2021</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">6</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">24</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">日被指使的服刑人从早上</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">7</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点许在五监区监舍</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">301</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">室被突然袭击踢落至昏迷，而将昏迷的伤瘫李碧云又在狱警的指挥下，被推到五监区的一车间的生产现场</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">D</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">线的墙边，抽着我前身一直将头部撞击墙身与又猛踢我双脚，头部被撞击到象爆炸一样，虽有知觉但喊不出音睁不开眼睛，手脚全身无力，动弹不得</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">,,,,,</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">我自醒来已近</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">12</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">点了，因头部被打伤严重，醒来想说话也发不出音，又不给治疗等，因我不能说话也写信投诉，不但没有纠正，还变本加历，</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">2021</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">年</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; mso-ligatures: none;">月</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">3</span><span style="color: #222222; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">号暴打我至腰椎再一次骨拆，也不同我去治疗，监狱警察应是保护服刑人员的生命安全的。但是内伤瘫李碧云在服刑期间受尽岐视非人性暴打迫害，都是被五监区陆娟警官违法滥用职权为得到</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">(</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">警号</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">4455551)</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">指使某些人有而为之暴打虐待折磨故意伤害身体，（<u>其喊</u></span><u><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">"</span></u><u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">刀下留人不要再打我受不住了等</span></u><u><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">"</span></u><u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span></u><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">旧伤未治好新伤三翻五次故而被伤害身体。使残病更加雪上加霜，生不如死，也得不到有效治疗。旧伤未治好新伤三翻五次故而被伤害身体。使残病更加雪上加霜，生不如死，也得不到对症治疗</span><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">。</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: Arial; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0cm; vertical-align: bottom;"><span style="color: #222222; font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Microsoft JhengHei&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-ligatures: none;">因我长时间被刑逼被注入慢性毒素，身体更差了，在</span><span lang="EN-GB" style="color: #222222;
